<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="English">English</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: English">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; font-size: 90%; background: #f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a> has articles on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/fil" class="extiw" title="w:fil">fil</a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/fil" class="extiw" title="w:fil">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">fil</strong> (<i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#uncountable" title="Appendix:Glossary">uncountable</a></i>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <a href="/wiki/Nordic" title="Nordic">Nordic</a> <a href="/wiki/dairy" title="dairy">dairy</a> product, similar to <a href="/wiki/yogurt" title="yogurt">yogurt</a>, but using different <a href="/wiki/bacteria" title="bacteria">bacteria</a> which give a different taste and texture.</li></ol>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Anagrams">Anagrams</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Anagrams">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/LIF#English" title="LIF">LIF</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/lif#English" title="lif">lif</a></span></li></ul>
<hr />

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar"><a href="/wiki/%D9%81%D9%8A%D9%84#Arabic" title="فيل">فِيل</a></i>&#8206; <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">fīl</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="az">fil</strong> (<i>definite accusative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-az def&#124;acc&#124;s-form-of" lang="az"><a href="/wiki/fili#Azerbaijani" title="fili">fili</a></b>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-az def&#124;p-form-of" lang="az"><a href="/wiki/fill%C9%99r#Azerbaijani" title="fillər">fillər</a></b>)
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Catalan">Catalan</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Catalan">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Occitan" class="extiw" title="w:Old Occitan">Old Occitan</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/filum#Latin" title="filum">fīlum</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/g%CA%B7%CA%B0iH-(s-)lo-&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/gʷʰiH-(s-)lo- (page does not exist)">*gʷʰiH-(s-)lo-</a></i>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Balearic_dialect" class="extiw" title="w:Balearic dialect">Balearic</a><span class="ib-comma qualifier-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Central_Catalan" class="extiw" title="w:Central Catalan">Central</a><span class="ib-comma qualifier-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Valencian" class="extiw" title="w:Valencian">Valencian</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Catalan_pronunciation" title="Appendix:Catalan pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>:&#32;<span class="IPA">/ˈfil/</span></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="ca">fil</strong>&#160;<span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-ca p-form-of" lang="ca"><a href="/wiki/fils#Catalan" title="fils">fils</a></b>)
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h2><span id="Norwegian_Bokm.C3.A5l"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Norwegian_Bokmål">Norwegian Bokmål</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=45" title="Edit section: Norwegian Bokmål">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_7">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=46" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_Bokm%C3%A5l_phonology" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Norwegian Bokmål phonology">key</a>)</sup>:&#32;<span class="IPA">/fiːl/</span></li>
<li>Rhymes: <a href="/w/index.php?title=Rhymes:Norwegian_Bokm%C3%A5l/i%CB%90l&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Rhymes:Norwegian Bokmål/iːl (page does not exist)"><span class="IPA">-iːl</span></a></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_11">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=47" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nb">fil</strong>&#160;<span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>definite singular</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nb"><a href="/wiki/fila#Norwegian_Bokmål" title="fila">fila</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nb"><a href="/wiki/filen#Norwegian_Bokmål" title="filen">filen</a></b>, <i>indefinite plural</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nb"><a href="/wiki/filer#Norwegian_Bokmål" title="filer">filer</a></b>, <i>definite plural</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nb"><a href="/wiki/filene#Norwegian_Bokmål" title="filene">filene</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <a href="/wiki/file" title="file">file</a>.</li>
<li>A hand tool used for removing sharp edges or for cutting, especially through metal.</li>
<li>A section of roadway for a single line of vehicles, a <a href="/wiki/lane" title="lane">lane</a>.</li></ol>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Old_French">Old French</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=50" title="Edit section: Old French">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=51" title="Edit section: Etymology 1">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/filium#Latin" title="filium">fīlium</a></i>, accusative singular of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/filius#Latin" title="filius">fīlius</a></i>. The nominative form <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href="/wiki/fiz#Old_French" title="fiz">fiz</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href="/wiki/fils#Old_French" title="fils">fils</a></i> (whence modern French <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href="/wiki/fils#French" title="fils">fils</a></i>), derives from the Latin nominative.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_8">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=52" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French_phonology" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Old French phonology">key</a>)</sup>:&#32;<span class="IPA">/fiʎ/</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_12">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=53" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="fro">fil</strong>&#160;<span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>oblique plural</i> <b class="Latn" lang="fro"><a href="/wiki/fiz#Old_French" title="fiz">fiz</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="fro"><a href="/wiki/filz#Old_French" title="filz">filz</a></b>, <i>nominative singular</i> <b class="Latn" lang="fro"><a href="/wiki/fiz#Old_French" title="fiz">fiz</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="fro"><a href="/wiki/filz#Old_French" title="filz">filz</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Latn" lang="fro"><strong class="selflink">fil</strong></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href="/wiki/son" title="son">son</a> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">male child</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_9">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=56" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French_phonology" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Old French phonology">key</a>)</sup>:&#32;<span class="IPA">/fil/</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_13">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=57" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="fro">fil</strong>&#160;<span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>oblique plural</i> <b class="Latn" lang="fro"><a href="/wiki/fis#Old_French" title="fis">fis</a></b>, <i>nominative singular</i> <b class="Latn" lang="fro"><a href="/wiki/fis#Old_French" title="fis">fis</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Latn" lang="fro"><strong class="selflink">fil</strong></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href="/wiki/thread" title="thread">thread</a> (fine strand of material)
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>circa 1170</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chr%C3%A9tien_de_Troyes" class="extiw" title="w:Chrétien de Troyes">Chrétien de Troyes</a>,  <cite>'<a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/fr:%C3%89rec_et_%C3%89nide" class="extiw" title="s:fr:Érec et Énide">Érec et Énide</a>'</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="fro">A <b>fil</b> d'or ovree et tissue.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">It was made and woven from fine threads of gold</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Descendants_3">Descendants</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=58" title="Edit section: Descendants">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<ul><li>French: <span class="Latn" lang="fr"><a href="/wiki/fil#French" title="fil">fil</a></span><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r54857417"/></li></ul>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Old_Irish">Old Irish</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=59" title="Edit section: Old Irish">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Alternative_forms">Alternative forms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=60" title="Edit section: Alternative forms">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="sga"><a href="/wiki/fail#Old_Irish" title="fail">fail</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="sga"><a href="/wiki/feil#Old_Irish" title="feil">feil</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="sga"><a href="/wiki/fel#Old_Irish" title="fel">fel</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="sga"><a href="/wiki/fele#Old_Irish" title="fele">fele</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="sga"><a href="/wiki/file#Old_Irish" title="file">file</a></span> (<i>relative</i>)</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=61" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Celtic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Celtic language">Proto-Celtic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="cel-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Celtic/wele&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Celtic/wele (page does not exist)">*wele</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">see!</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the imperative of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Celtic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Celtic language">Proto-Celtic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="cel-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Celtic/weleti" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Celtic/weleti">*weleti</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">see</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/wel-" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/wel-">*wel-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">see</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Welsh_language" class="extiw" title="w:Welsh language">Welsh</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cy"><a href="/wiki/gweled#Welsh" title="gweled">gweled</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to see</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Semantic development from "see!" to "there is" is parallel to that of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href="/wiki/voici#French" title="voici">voici</a></i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">vois ci</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">see here</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href="/wiki/voil%C3%A0#French" title="voilà">voilà</a></i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">vois là</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">see there</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_10">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=62" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Old_Irish_pronunciation" title="Appendix:Old Irish pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>:&#32;<span class="IPA">/fʲilʲ/</span></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=63" title="Edit section: Verb">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="sga">·fil</strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#present_tense" title="Appendix:Glossary">present</a> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#progressive" title="Appendix:Glossary">progressive</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/conjunct" class="extiw" title="w:conjunct">conjunct</a> of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="sga"><a href="/wiki/att%C3%A1#Old_Irish" title="attá">at·tá</a></i></span></span>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#c." title="Appendix:Glossary">c.</a></i> <b>800</b>, Würzburg Glosses on the Pauline Epistles, published in <i>Thesaurus Palaeohibernicus</i> (reprinted 1987, Dublin Institute for Advanced Studies), edited and with translations by Whitley Stokes and John Strachan, vol.&#160;I, pp.&#160;499–712,&#32;Wb. 19<small><small style="position:relative;top:-.5em">c</small></small>20
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="sga">Má nudub<b>·feil</b> i n‑ellug coirp Críst, adib cland Abrache amal ṡodin, <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">et</i> it sib ata chomarpi Abracham.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">If you <span class="gender"><abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> are in the union of the body of Christ, you are Abraham’s children in that case, and it is you who are Abraham’s heirs.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="sga">fil</strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#third_person" title="Appendix:Glossary">third-person</a> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#singular_number" title="Appendix:Glossary">singular</a> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#present_tense" title="Appendix:Glossary">present</a> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#progressive" title="Appendix:Glossary">progressive</a> <a href="/wiki/relative" title="relative">relative</a> of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="sga"><a href="/wiki/att%C3%A1#Old_Irish" title="attá">at·tá</a></i></span></span>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#c." title="Appendix:Glossary">c.</a></i> <b>875</b>, Milan Glosses on the Psalms, published in <i>Thesaurus Palaeohibernicus</i> (reprinted 1987, Dublin Institute for Advanced Studies), edited and with translations by Whitley Stokes and John Strachan, vol.&#160;I, pp.&#160;7–483,&#32;Ml. 114<small><small style="position:relative;top:-.5em">b</small></small>18
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="sga">nád <b>fil</b> nech con·gné fris ón acht Día</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">that there is no one to help him but God</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=64" title="Edit section: Usage notes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>In the conjunct form, the logical subject appears in the accusative (or as an infixed object pronoun) in the oldest language. Examples: <i class="Latn mention" lang="sga"><a href="/w/index.php?title=n%C3%ADconfil&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="níconfil (page does not exist)">nícon·ḟil</a> <a href="/wiki/nach#Old_Irish" title="nach">nach</a> <a href="/wiki/rainn#Old_Irish" title="rainn">rainn</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">there is no part</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="sga"><a href="/w/index.php?title=n%C3%ADnfil&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="nínfil (page does not exist)">nín·fil</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">we are not</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="sga"><a href="/w/index.php?title=condibfeil&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="condibfeil (page does not exist)">condib·feil</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">so that you <span class="gender"><abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> are</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=67" title="Edit section: Serbo-Croatian">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Alternative_forms_2">Alternative forms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=68" title="Edit section: Alternative forms">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="sh"><a href="/w/index.php?title=filj&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="filj (page does not exist)">fȉlj</a></span></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_6">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=69" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ottoman_Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ottoman Turkish language">Ottoman Turkish</a></span> <i class="ota-Arab mention" lang="ota"><a href="/wiki/%D9%81%DB%8C%D9%84#Ottoman_Turkish" title="فیل">فیل</a></i>&#8206; <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ota-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">fil</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (modern Turkish <i class="Latn mention" lang="tr"><a href="/wiki/fil#Turkish" title="fil">fil</a></i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar"><a href="/wiki/%D9%81%D9%8A%D9%84#Arabic" title="فيل">فِيل</a></i>&#8206; <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">fīl</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Persian" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Persian">Middle Persian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pal"><a href="/wiki/pyl#Middle_Persian" title="pyl">pyl</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="pal-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pīl</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Akkadian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Akkadian language">Akkadian</a></span> <i class="Xsux mention" lang="akk"><a href="/wiki/%F0%92%84%A0%F0%92%8B%9B#Akkadian" title="𒄠𒋛">𒄠𒋛</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="akk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pīru</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Akin to <i class="Latn mention" lang="sh"><a href="/wiki/fildi%C5%A1#Serbo-Croatian" title="fildiš">fìldiš</a></i>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_11">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=70" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">fȉl</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>: <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Serbo-Croatian_pronunciation" title="Appendix:Serbo-Croatian pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>:&#32;<span class="IPA">/fîl/</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">fȋl</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>: <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Serbo-Croatian_pronunciation" title="Appendix:Serbo-Croatian pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>:&#32;<span class="IPA">/fîːl/</span></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_14">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=71" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="sh">fȉl</strong>&#160;<span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>Cyrillic spelling</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="sh"><a href="/wiki/%D1%84%D0%B8%D0%BB#Serbo-Croatian" title="фил">фи̏л</a></b>) <i>or</i>
<strong class="Latn headword" lang="sh">fȋl</strong>&#160;<span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>Cyrillic spelling</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="sh"><a href="/wiki/%D1%84%D0%B8%D0%BB#Serbo-Croatian" title="фил">фи̑л</a></b>)

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Swedish">Swedish</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=75" title="Edit section: Swedish">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_3">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=76" title="Edit section: Etymology 1">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml"><a href="/wiki/vile#Middle_Low_German" title="vile">vīle</a></i>.
Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/file#English" title="file">file</a></i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href="/wiki/Feile#German" title="Feile">Feile</a></i>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_12">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=77" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_15">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=78" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="sv">fil</strong>&#160;<span class="gender"><abbr title="common gender">c</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>a <a href="/wiki/file" title="file">file</a> (a tool)</li></ol>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_4">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=81" title="Edit section: Etymology 2">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: #777777;">(This <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:Etymology" title="Wiktionary:Etymology">etymology</a> is missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:Etymology_scriptorium" title="Wiktionary:Etymology scriptorium">Etymology scriptorium</a>. Particularly: “French <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href="/wiki/file#French" title="file">file</a></i>?”)</span>.
</p><p>Row and lane (a row of vehicles) is one etymology, but as English <a href="/wiki/file" title="file">file</a> suggests computer file has a different etymology. However, the Swedish computer file is sometimes explained as a row of bytes, in attempt to shoehorn this new English loanword into the etymology of the existing word.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_13">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=82" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Swedish_pronunciation" title="Appendix:Swedish pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>:&#32;<span class="IPA">/fiːl/</span></li>
<li><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r50165410"/><table class="audiotable" style="vertical-align: bottom; display:inline-block; list-style:none;line-height: 1em; border-collapse:collapse;"><tbody><tr><td class="unicode audiolink" style="padding-right:5px; padding-left: 0;">audio</td><td class="audiofile"><div class="mediaContainer" style="width:175px"><audio id="mwe_player_2" controls="" preload="none" style="width:175px" class="kskin" data-durationhint="1.3" data-startoffset="0" data-mwtitle="Sv-fil.ogg" data-mwprovider="wikimediacommons"><source src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/f/f3/Sv-fil.ogg" type="audio/ogg; codecs=&quot;vorbis&quot;" data-title="Original Ogg file (101 kbps)" data-shorttitle="Ogg source" data-width="0" data-height="0" data-bandwidth="101015" /><source src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/transcoded/f/f3/Sv-fil.ogg/Sv-fil.ogg.mp3" type="audio/mpeg" data-title="MP3" data-shorttitle="MP3" data-transcodekey="mp3" data-width="0" data-height="0" data-bandwidth="140176" /></audio></div></td><td class="audiometa" style="font-size: 80%;">(<a href="/wiki/File:Sv-fil.ogg" title="File:Sv-fil.ogg">file</a>)</td></tr></tbody></table></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_16">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=83" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="sv">fil</strong>&#160;<span class="gender"><abbr title="common gender">c</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>a row of objects; most commonly used about moving objects</li>
<li>a section of roadway for a single line of vehicles, a <a href="/wiki/lane" title="lane">lane</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/file" title="file">file</a> (in computer technology)</li></ol>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_17">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=88" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="sv">fil</strong>&#160;<span class="gender"><abbr title="common gender">c</abbr></span> (<i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#uncountable" title="Appendix:Glossary">uncountable</a></i>)
</p>
<ol><li>any product from a family of various (deliberately) soured milk products</li>
<li>abbreviation for <i><a href="/wiki/filmj%C3%B6lk" title="filmjölk">filmjölk</a></i>; a particular kind of <i>fil</i> as above</li></ol>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Turkish">Turkish</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=96" title="Edit section: Turkish">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_8">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=97" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ottoman_Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ottoman Turkish language">Ottoman Turkish</a></span> <i class="ota-Arab mention" lang="ota"><a href="/wiki/%D9%81%DB%8C%D9%84#Ottoman_Turkish" title="فیل">فیل</a></i>&#8206; <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ota-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">fil</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar"><a href="/wiki/%D9%81%D9%8A%D9%84#Arabic" title="فيل">فِيل</a></i>&#8206; <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">fīl</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa"><a href="/wiki/%D9%BE%DB%8C%D9%84#Persian" title="پیل">پیل</a></i>&#8206; <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pīl</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (and from alternate <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ottoman_Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ottoman Turkish language">Ottoman Turkish</a></span> <i class="ota-Arab mention" lang="ota"><a href="/wiki/%D9%BE%DB%8C%D9%84#Ottoman_Turkish" title="پیل">پیل</a></i>&#8206; <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ota-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pil</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, directly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa"><a href="/wiki/%D9%BE%DB%8C%D9%84#Persian" title="پیل">پیل</a></i>&#8206; <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pīl</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Akkadian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Akkadian language">Akkadian</a></span> <i class="Xsux mention" lang="akk"><a href="/wiki/%F0%92%84%A0%F0%92%8B%9B#Akkadian" title="𒄠𒋛">𒄠𒋛</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="akk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pīru</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Egyptian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Egyptian language">Egyptian</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="egy"><a href="/wiki/%EA%9C%A3bw#Egyptian" title="ꜣbw">ꜣbw</a></i> (root of English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/elephant#English" title="elephant">elephant</a></i>).
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_15">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=98" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Turkish_pronunciation" title="Appendix:Turkish pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>:&#32;<span class="IPA">/fil/</span></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_19">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=99" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="tr">fil</strong> (<i>definite accusative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-tr def&#124;acc&#124;s-form-of" lang="tr"><a href="/wiki/fili#Turkish" title="fili">fili</a></b>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-tr p-form-of" lang="tr"><a href="/wiki/filler#Turkish" title="filler">filler</a></b>)
